List of awesome open source applications for macOS. This list contains a lot of native, and cross-platform apps. The main goal of this repository is to find free open source apps and start contributing. Feel free to [contribute](origin/CONTRIBUTING.md) to the list, any suggestions are welcome!

To receive all new or popular applications you can join our [telegram channel](https://t.me/opensourcemacosapps).

## Support
